        WHERE ([f].[HomeTeamId] = @__8__locals2_homeTeam_ClubId_0 AND [f].[AwayTeamId] = @__awayTeam_ClubId_1) OR ([f].[HomeTeamId] = @__awayTeam_ClubId_1 AND [f].[AwayTeamId] = @__8__locals2_homeTeam_ClubId_0)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
